### [166] [Privileged Foresight Distillation: Zero-Cost Future Correction for World Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25859)
*Pengcheng Fang,Hongli Chen,Xiaohao Cai*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出特权前瞻蒸馏（PFD），将世界动作模型中未来信息的角色从预测目标或正则化器重新定义为可压缩的校正，通过蒸馏未来条件校正到仅使用当前帧的策略中，提升操作性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界动作模型联合训练未来视频预测和动作预测，但研究发现推理时可移除未来预测分支而性能损失很小，这引发疑问：未来信息究竟扮演什么角色？作者认为未来信息在动作去噪中提供了特权校正，而当前仅策略只能部分捕捉这种校正。

Method: 提出特权前瞻蒸馏（PFD），将特权前瞻（真实未来与仅当前帧预测之间的动作去噪方向残差）从训练时的教师模型蒸馏到仅使用当前帧的学生模型的小型适配器中。教师和学生共享相同骨干网络，仅在视频token的注意力掩码上不同，推理时从不生成未来视频。

Result: 控制实验验证了性能提升确实来自未来条件校正，而非容量或正则化的副作用。在LIBERO和RoboTwin操作基准测试中，PFD实现了持续改进，同时保持了仅当前帧的推理接口，额外延迟可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 该研究重新定义了世界动作模型中未来信息的作用：不是要预测的目标，也不是要吸收的正则化器，而是可压缩的、需要蒸馏的校正。PFD方法成功将特权未来信息转化为可操作的性能提升。

Abstract: World action models jointly predict future video and action during training, raising an open question about what role the future-prediction branch actually plays. A recent finding shows that this branch can be removed at inference with little to no loss on common manipulation benchmarks, suggesting that future information may act merely as a regularizer on the shared visual backbone. We propose instead that joint training induces an action-conditioned correction that privileged future observations impose on action denoising, and that current-only policies capture this correction only partially. Making the account precise, we formulate privileged foresight as a residual in the action-denoising direction -- the difference between what a model predicts given the true future and what it predicts given only the current frame -- and introduce \emph{Privileged Foresight Distillation (PFD)}, which transfers this residual from a training-time teacher into a small adapter on a current-only student. The teacher and student share the same backbone and differ only in the attention mask over video tokens; future video is never generated at inference. Controlled experiments verify that this gain reflects a genuine future-conditioned correction rather than a side effect of capacity or regularization. Empirically, PFD achieves consistent improvements on LIBERO and RoboTwin manipulation benchmarks while preserving the current-only inference interface at negligible added latency. This view reframes the role of future information in world action models: not as a target to predict, nor as a regularizer to absorb, but as a compressible correction to be distilled.

</details>


### [167] [Variational Neural Belief Parameterizations for Robust Dexterous Grasping under Multimodal Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.25897)
*Clinton Enwerem,Shreya Kalyanaraman,John S. Baras,Calin Belta*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于变分推理的抓取规划方法，使用可微分高斯混合模型表示信念，通过Gumbel-Softmax组件选择和重参数化技术优化条件风险价值(CVaR)，提高抓取在接触不确定性和外部扰动下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于期望质量的抓取规划方法忽略了尾部风险，在不利接触情况下容易失败。现有的风险敏感POMDP方法使用粒子滤波信念，存在扩展性差、阻碍梯度优化、CVaR估计方差高等问题。

Method: 将抓取获取建模为潜在接触参数和物体姿态的变分推理问题，使用可微分高斯混合模型表示信念。采用Gumbel-Softmax组件选择和位置-尺度重参数化技术，使样本成为信念参数的光滑函数，从而通过可微分CVaR代理实现路径梯度，直接优化尾部鲁棒性。

Result: 在仿真中，该方法在接触参数不确定性和外部力扰动下提高了鲁棒抓取成功率，规划时间比粒子滤波模型预测控制减少约一个数量级。在实际机器人实验中，相比高斯基线方法，控制器在更少步骤和更短时间内完成，获得更高的触觉抓取质量代理值，风险校准更准确。

Conclusion: 提出的变分神经信念方法能够有效处理抓取执行中的随机性，通过可微分CVaR优化提高尾部鲁棒性，在保持高成功率的同时显著减少计算时间，为不确定环境下的机器人抓取提供了一种高效的风险感知解决方案。

Abstract: Contact variability, sensing uncertainty, and external disturbances make grasp execution stochastic. Expected-quality objectives ignore tail outcomes and often select grasps that fail under adverse contact realizations. Risk-sensitive POMDPs address this failure mode, but many use particle-filter beliefs that scale poorly, obstruct gradient-based optimization, and estimate Conditional Value-at-Risk (CVaR) with high-variance approximations. We instead formulate grasp acquisition as variational inference over latent contact parameters and object pose, representing the belief with a differentiable Gaussian mixture. We use Gumbel-Softmax component selection and location-scale reparameterization to express samples as smooth functions of the belief parameters, enabling pathwise gradients through a differentiable CVaR surrogate for direct optimization of tail robustness. In simulation, our variational neural belief improves robust grasp success under contact-parameter uncertainty and exogenous force perturbations while reducing planning time by roughly an order of magnitude relative to particle-filter model-predictive control. On a serial-chain robot arm with a multifingered hand, we validate grasp-and-lift success under object-pose uncertainty against a Gaussian baseline. Both methods succeed on the tested perturbations, but our controller terminates in fewer steps and less wall-clock time while achieving a higher tactile grasp-quality proxy. Our learned belief also calibrates risk more accurately, keeping mean absolute calibration error below 0.14 across tested simulation regimes, compared with 0.58 for a Cross-Entropy Method planner.

</details>
